class \mbox{\hyperlink{classtesseract__planning_1_1SimpleMotionPlanner}{Simple\+Motion\+Planner}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em The simple planner is meant to be a tool for assigning values to the seed. The planner simply loops over all of the Move\+Instructions and then calls the appropriate function from the profile. These functions do not depend on the seed, so this may be used to initialize the seed appropriately using e.\+g. linear interpolation. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacetesseract__planning_a97a7a198edf46fea10c33898f4b1e2c5}\label{namespacetesseract__planning_a97a7a198edf46fea10c33898f4b1e2c5}} 
\index{tesseract\_planning@{tesseract\_planning}!PlannerProfileRemapping@{PlannerProfileRemapping}}
\index{PlannerProfileRemapping@{PlannerProfileRemapping}!tesseract\_planning@{tesseract\_planning}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{PlannerProfileRemapping}{PlannerProfileRemapping}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily using \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetesseract__planning_a97a7a198edf46fea10c33898f4b1e2c5}{tesseract\+\_\+planning\+::\+Planner\+Profile\+Remapping}} = typedef std\+::unordered\+\_\+map$<$std\+::string, std\+::unordered\+\_\+map$<$std\+::string, std\+::string$>$ $>$}

This used to store planner specific profile mapping with the request

For example say you have a profile named Raster in your command language. Say you have multiple Raster profiles for descartes \{Raster, Raster1, Raster2\}. This allows you to remap the meaning of Raster in the command language to say Raster2 for the specific planner Descartes by Map$<$\+Descartes, Map$<$\+Raster, Raster1$>$$>$. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacetesseract__planning_ae98ce6e841caa404388d1689b4ffe1db}\label{namespacetesseract__planning_ae98ce6e841caa404388d1689b4ffe1db}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum class \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetesseract__planning_adc15a5456ea446dfa3dc95852bc9d579}{tesseract\+\_\+planning\+::\+Robot\+Config}}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [strong]}}



The Robot\+Config enum. 

The first letter refers to \textquotesingle{}Flip vs No-\/\+Flip\textquotesingle{}, think of the human arm as the robot this would relate to wrist flipped or not flipped.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Which is indicated by flipping the sign of J5 requiring J4 and J6 to move by +/-\/180 degrees The second letter refers to \textquotesingle{}Up vs Down\textquotesingle{} think of the human arm as the robot this would relate to elbow up or down
\item Which is indicated, J3 is greater than or less than 90 degrees and tool0 position x is positive or negative The third letter refers to \textquotesingle{}Front vs Back\textquotesingle{} think of the human arm as the robot this would relate to arm in front or back 
\end{DoxyItemize}\begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}

Check the waypoints joint order against the provided joint names. 

Throws if waypoint does not directly contain that information

\index{tesseract\_planning@{tesseract\_planning}!interpolateCartCartWaypoint@{interpolateCartCartWaypoint}}
\index{interpolateCartCartWaypoint@{interpolateCartCartWaypoint}!tesseract\_planning@{tesseract\_planning}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{interpolateCartCartWaypoint()}{interpolateCartCartWaypoint()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily std\+::vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structtesseract__planning_1_1MoveInstructionPoly}{Move\+Instruction\+Poly}} $>$ tesseract\+\_\+planning\+::interpolate\+Cart\+Cart\+Waypoint (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structtesseract__planning_1_1JointGroupInstructionInfo}{Joint\+Group\+Instruction\+Info}} \&}]{prev,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structtesseract__planning_1_1JointGroupInstructionInfo}{Joint\+Group\+Instruction\+Info}} \&}]{base,  }\item[{double}]{state\+\_\+lvs\+\_\+length,  }\item[{double}]{translation\+\_\+lvs\+\_\+length,  }\item[{double}]{rotation\+\_\+lvs\+\_\+length,  }\item[{int}]{min\+\_\+steps,  }\item[{int}]{max\+\_\+steps,  }\item[{const tesseract\+\_\+scene\+\_\+graph\+::\+Scene\+State \&}]{scene\+\_\+state }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



\mbox{\hyperlink{classtesseract__planning_1_1CartesianWaypoint}{Cartesian\+Waypoint}} to \mbox{\hyperlink{classtesseract__planning_1_1CartesianWaypoint}{Cartesian\+Waypoint}}. 

This does not include the prev instruction but does include the base instruction

This function interpolates the motion from start state to end state.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item the number of steps for the plan will be calculated such that\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item the translation distance between successive steps is no longer than translation\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment
\item the rotational distance between successive steps is no longer than rotation\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment
\item the number of steps for the plan will be calculated such that the norm of all joint distances between successive steps is no longer than state\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment\+\_\+length
\item the max steps from the above calculations will be be compared to the min\+\_\+steps and the largest will be chosen
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item the interpolation will be done based on the condition below
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Case 1\+: Joint solution found for start and end cartesian waypoint
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item It interpolates the joint position from the start to the end state
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Case 2\+: Joint solution only found for start cartesian waypoint
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item It creates number states based on the steps and sets the value to found start solution
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Case 3\+: Joint solution only found for end cartesian waypoint
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item It creates number states based on the steps and sets the value to found end solution
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Case 4\+: No joint solution found for end and start cartesian waypoint
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item It creates number states based on the steps and sets the value to the current state of the environment
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em state\+\_\+lvs\+\_\+length} & The maximum joint distance, the norm of changes to all joint positions between successive steps. \\
\hline
{\em translation\+\_\+lvs\+\_\+length} & The maximum translation distance between successive steps \\
\hline
{\em rotation\+\_\+lvs\+\_\+length} & The maximum rotational distance between successive steps \\
\hline
{\em min\+\_\+steps} & The minimum number of steps for the plan \\
\hline
{\em max\+\_\+steps} & The maximum number of steps for the plan \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A vector of move instruction 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacetesseract__planning_a0696dcbe6dc69b1e15c4ab36a43bffc8}\label{namespacetesseract__planning_a0696dcbe6dc69b1e15c4ab36a43bffc8}}

This function interpolates the motion from start state to end state.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item the number of steps for the plan will be calculated such that\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item the translation distance between successive steps is no longer than translation\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment
\item the rotational distance between successive steps is no longer than rotation\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment
\item the number of steps for the plan will be calculated such that the norm of all joint distances between successive steps is no longer than state\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment\+\_\+length

\end{DoxyItemize}

\end{DoxyItemize}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{interpolateCartJointWaypoint()}{interpolateCartJointWaypoint()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily std\+::vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structtesseract__planning_1_1MoveInstructionPoly}{Move\+Instruction\+Poly}} $>$ tesseract\+\_\+planning\+::interpolate\+Cart\+Joint\+Waypoint (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structtesseract__planning_1_1KinematicGroupInstructionInfo}{Kinematic\+Group\+Instruction\+Info}} \&}]{prev,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structtesseract__planning_1_1KinematicGroupInstructionInfo}{Kinematic\+Group\+Instruction\+Info}} \&}]{base,  }\item[{double}]{state\+\_\+lvs\+\_\+length,  }\item[{double}]{translation\+\_\+lvs\+\_\+length,  }\item[{double}]{rotation\+\_\+lvs\+\_\+length,  }\item[{int}]{min\+\_\+steps,  }\item[{int}]{max\+\_\+steps }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



\mbox{\hyperlink{classtesseract__planning_1_1CartesianWaypoint}{Cartesian\+Waypoint}} to \mbox{\hyperlink{classtesseract__planning_1_1JointWaypoint}{Joint\+Waypoint}}. 

This does not include the prev instruction but does include the base instruction

This function interpolates the motion from start state to end state.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item the number of steps for the plan will be calculated such that\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item the translation distance between successive steps is no longer than translation\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment
\item the rotational distance between successive steps is no longer than rotation\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment
\item the number of steps for the plan will be calculated such that the norm of all joint distances between successive steps is no longer than state\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment\+\_\+length
\item the max steps from the above calculations will be be compared to the min\+\_\+steps and the largest will be chosen
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item the interpolation will be done based on the condition below
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Case 1\+: Joint solution found for start cartesian waypoint
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item It interpolates the joint position from the start to the end state
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Case 2\+: Unable to find joint solution for start cartesian waypoint
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item It creates number states based on the steps and sets the value to end joint waypoint
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em state\+\_\+lvs\+\_\+length} & The maximum joint distance, the norm of changes to all joint positions between successive steps. \\
\hline
{\em translation\+\_\+lvs\+\_\+length} & The maximum translation distance between successive steps \\
\hline
{\em rotation\+\_\+lvs\+\_\+length} & The maximum rotational distance between successive steps \\
\hline
{\em min\+\_\+steps} & The minimum number of steps for the plan \\
\hline
{\em max\+\_\+steps} & The maximum number of steps for the plan \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A vector of move instruction 
\end{DoxyReturn}
